b=#branches n=#nodes l=#loops  ^ucvXgzFo

%%***>>>text element-link:[[Superposition Theorem]]<<<***%%Superposition Theorem ^d732IpCt

To find the voltage (  ) ^LyyncxcX

across    : 1. Find voltage v1 across R2 due 
to voltage source only 2. Find voltage v2
across R2 due to current source only. Repeat
for each. Vt = V1 + V2. Voltage source is
